type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v,

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(e1,

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(e1, e2) => Ap

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(e1, e2) => Ap(subst(

type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

                       then Lam(y, e1)

        | Ap(e1, e2) => Ap(subst(v, x, e1) ,

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(e1, e2) => Ap(subst(v, x, e1) , subst(

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(e1, e2) => Ap(subst(v, x, e1) , subst(v,

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(e1, e2) => Ap(subst(v, x, e1) , subst(v, x,

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(e1, e2) => Ap(subst(v, x, e1) , subst(v, x, e2

# A simplified lambda calculus expression containing variables, lambdas, and applications #
type Exp =
  + Var(String)
  + Lam(String, Exp)
  + Ap(Exp, Exp)
in

# Substitute Exp v for variable name in Exp e #
let subst: (Exp, String, Exp) -> Exp =
    fun v, x, e ->
        case e
        | Var(y) => if y 
                    then v
                    else Var(x)
        | Lam(y, e1) => if y 
                       then Lam(y, e1)
                       else Lam(x, subst(v, x, e1) )
        | Ap(e1, e2) => Ap(subst(v, x, e1) , subst(v, x, e2) ) end
